rm -f img.o output.o main.o fail.o input.o compute.o heat_omp_static
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c img.c -o img.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c output.c -o output.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c main.c -o main.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c fail.c -o fail.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c input.c -o input.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include -c compute.c -o compute.o 	
gcc -O2 -std=gnu99 -fopenmp -I../../include img.o output.o main.o fail.o input.o compute.o -o heat_omp_static

  -p 1 # number of threads (if applicable)
  -r 0 # print intermediate reports every reduction cycle
